msg:My stay at Wutong Apartments was wonderful! The room was clean, spacious, modern, and aesthetically pleasing. There is bathtub is luxurious and spacious, the shower  has great pressure and the the separate toilet room has a motion censored toilet seat and a bidet. The bed was comfy and the closet space begs you to unpack your suitcase. There were thoughtful amenities, including a loofah cloth and shoe shine cloths. Now...the breakfast. It was the best breakfast buffet I've ever had the pleasure of experiencing. Tinder and well seasoned steak, salmon, soups, desserts, breads, scrumptious pancakes and a salad bar that even included kale amongst the varied greens. Best of all, the service was exceptional. A special thank you to Li Ne, the dining staff and the housekeeper who attended to my room. I wish that every hotel stay I experience in the future is as amazing as my time at Wutong Apartment Hotel.

I was very surprised and moved by the service, with full marks for the details. There is a staff member at the gate to help carry the luggage. After check-in, the staff will use a cart to deliver the luggage to the room. When taking the elevator, they will help to press the elevator. Every time you travel, you can hear the staff say "Hello" kindly. After check-in, the hotel warmly presented a fruit plate, hot white fungus soup to warm up and snacks.
This time I stayed in the hotel for a long time. Every time I leave the hotel and come back, the room is tidied up, my personal belongings are placed in an orderly manner, the clothes are neatly folded, and the dirty socks scattered on the floor are washed by the waiter and dried by hand. , Contact the hotel staff for the dirty clothes that have been worn, and they will come to your door for dry cleaning.
Before I checked in, I asked the front desk, "Why is it called Wutong Apar**ent? Instead of Wutong Hotel?" The reply was "Because the hotel's decoration style is close to apar**ent style, and I want to give the guests a feeling of going home."
Indeed, very warm, like "the feeling of coming home". Next time I have a chance, this hotel must be the best choice in my heart.
